Modern Decklists
================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on September 3, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/author_Gleeson.jpg)
By Chris Gleeson




 Chris is the copy editor for DailyMTG. If the Ts are dotted and the eyes are crossed, he dun goofed. 






These are all 24 of the decklists registered for Modern by the competitors at the 2016 *Magic* World Championship.







#### Lukas Blohon: Scapeshift


#####
